         	define("vr.tpl445",["$s","$"],function($s,$){

	function imageFactory(item, width, height){
		var w = item.width;
		var h = item.height;
		var img = document.createElement("img");
		img.style.position = "relative";

		var dh = width/w*h;
		if(dh > height){
			img.style.width = width+"px";
			img.style.height = dh+"px";
			img.style.top = (height-dh)/2+"px";
		}
		else{
			img.style.height = height+"px";
			var dw = height/h*w;
			img.style.width = dw+"px";
			img.style.left = (width-dw)/2+"px";
		}
		return img;
	}

	function getPic(picarr, start, width, piclist,classId,rank){

		var height = 120, para1 = 135, para2 = 35000;
		var end = start;

		var _width = width*1.1;
		var diff = _width, sum = 0;

		for(var i=start;i<picarr.length;i++){
			var item = picarr[i];
			var w = item.width/(item.height/height);
			var d = diff - w;
			if(Math.abs(d) < Math.abs(diff)){
				diff = diff - w;
				sum += w;
			}
			else{
				end = i-1;
				break;
			}
		}

		if(i == picarr.length) end = picarr.length-1;

		var finW = width-(end-start+2);
		var _sum = 0;

		var rate = finW/sum;
		for(var i=start;i<=end;i++){
		var item = picarr[i];
			var li = document.createElement("li");
			var link = document.createElement("a");
			if(item.imageTag!=''){
				var span=document.createElement('span');
				var span2=document.createElement('span');
				span.setAttribute('size','small');
				span2.setAttribute('size','big');
				span.setAttribute('class','pictotal');
				span2.setAttribute('class','pictotal');
				span.innerHTML=item.imageTag;
				span2.innerHTML=item.imageTag;
			}
			var w = item.width/(item.height/height);
			w = Math.round(w * rate);
			if(i==end){
				w = finW - _sum;
			}
			_sum += w;
			var h = height * rate;
			h = h>height?height:h;

			link.setAttribute("target","_blank");
			link.setAttribute("href",item.link);
			link.setAttribute("id","sogou_vr_"+classId+"_small_"+rank);
			link.style.zIndex = 1;
			link.style.overflow = "hidden";
			link.style.display = "block";
			link.style.height = h+"px";

			li.style.position = "relative";
			li.style.width = w+"px";
			li.style.height = h+"px";

			var img = imageFactory(item, w, h);
			img.setAttribute("src",item.src.replace(/img(\d+)\.store\.sogou\.com/g,'img$1.sogoucdn.com'));
			img.setAttribute("style","width:"+w+"px;height:"+h+"px;top:0px;left:0px;");
			img.style.zIndex = 1;
			link.appendChild(img);
			if(item.imageTag!=''){link.appendChild(span)}
			li.appendChild(link);

			var pop_width = w*1.25+"px";
			var pop_height = h*1.25+"px";
			var pop_left = (0-w*0.1)+"px";
			var pop_top = (0-h*0.1)+"px";

			var link2 = document.createElement("a");
			link2.setAttribute("target","_blank");
			link2.setAttribute("href",item.link);
	if(item.imageTag!=''){
		link2.setAttribute("id","sogou_vr_"+classId+"_small_360_"+rank);
	}else{
		link2.setAttribute("id","sogou_vr_"+classId+"_small_"+rank);
	}

      link2.setAttribute("style","display:none;position:absolute;width:"+pop_width+";height:"+pop_height+";top:"+pop_top+";left:"+pop_left+";");
      link2.setAttribute("pop_width",pop_width);
	    link2.setAttribute("pop_height",pop_height);
	    link2.setAttribute("pop_left",pop_left);
	    link2.setAttribute("pop_top",pop_top);

		 link2.setAttribute("back_width",w+'px');
	    link2.setAttribute("back_height",h+'px');

	    link2.style.display = "none";

			var img2 = imageFactory(item, w, h);
			img2.setAttribute("src",item.src.replace(/img(\d+)\.store\.sogou\.com/g,'img$1.sogoucdn.com'));
			img2.setAttribute("style","display:none;position:absolute;width:"+w+"px;height:"+h+"px;top:0px;left:0px;");
			img2.style.display = "none";
			link2.appendChild(img2);
			if(item.imageTag!=''){link2.appendChild(span2)}
			li.appendChild(link2);
			piclist.appendChild(li);

			if(item.imageTag!=''){
				var param = {"backLink":link,"backImage":img,'backspan':span,'popspan':span2,"popLink":link2,"popImage":img2,"parentLi":li};
			}else{
				var param = {"backLink":link,"backImage":img,"popLink":link2,"popImage":img2,"parentLi":li};
			}
			var userAgent = window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			if(!(/msie 6\.0/i.test(userAgent) || /msie 7\.0/i.test(userAgent)))
				$(li).bind("mouseenter",param,showPop).bind("mouseleave",param,hidePop);
		}
		return {index:end+1,height:h};
	}

	function showPop(event){
        	var backLink = event.data.backLink;
			var backImage = event.data.backImage;
			var popLink = event.data.popLink;
			var popImage = event.data.popImage;
			var parentLi =  event.data.parentLi;

			var pop_width = popLink.getAttribute("pop_width");
			var pop_height = popLink.getAttribute("pop_height")
			var pop_top = popLink.getAttribute("pop_top");
			var pop_left = popLink.getAttribute("pop_left");

			var back_width=parseInt(popLink.getAttribute('back_width'));
			var back_height=parseInt(popLink.getAttribute('back_height'));
			var popspan;
			if(event.data.popspan){
				popspan=event.data.popspan;
				popspan.style.zIndex=99;
				popspan.style.right = (parseInt(pop_width)-back_width)/2+'px';
				popspan.style.bottom = (parseInt(pop_height)-back_height)/2+'px';
			}

			popLink.style.width = pop_width;
			popLink.style.height = pop_height;
			popLink.style.left = pop_left;
			popLink.style.top = pop_top;
			popLink.style.zIndex = 99;

			popImage.style.left = pop_left.substr(1);
			popImage.style.top = pop_top.substr(1);
			popImage.style.width = backImage.style.width;
			popImage.style.height = backImage.style.height;



			backLink.style.display = "none";
			backImage.style.display = "none";
			popLink.style.display = "";
			popImage.style.display = ""

        if(!/msie/i.test(window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase()))
        {
            popImage.style.position = "absolute";
            try{
                $(popLink).animate({
                    width:pop_width,
                    height:pop_height,
                    left:pop_left,
                    top:pop_top
                },200);
                $(popImage).animate({
                    width:pop_width,
                    height:pop_height,
                    left:"0px",
                    top:"0px"
                },200);
				if(event.data.popspan){
					$(popspan).animate({
						right:'0px',
						bottom:'0px'
					},200)
				}
            }catch(e){
                popImage.style.width = pop_width;
                popImage.style.height = pop_height;
                popImage.style.left = "0px";
                popImage.style.top = "0px";
                $(popLink).aminate({
                    width:pop_width,
                    height:pop_height,
                    left:pop_left,
                    top:pop_top
                },200);
            }
        }else{
            $(popImage).animate({
                width:pop_width,
                height:pop_height,
                left:"0px",
                top:"0px"
            },200);
			if(event.data.popspan){
					$(popspan).animate({
						right:'0px',
						bottom:'0px'
					},200)
				}
        }
        popImage.style.zIndex = 99;
        parentLi.style.zIndex = 99;
    }


	
	
			
			
			
			
			



			
			
			
			

			
			
			
			
			

			
			
			
			

			
			
			
			


			
			
			  
				
			  
			  
			  
			
				
						
						
						
						
					
			



			
			

  


  function hidePop(event){
			var backLink = event.data.backLink;
			var backImage = event.data.backImage;
			var popLink = event.data.popLink;
			var popImage = event.data.popImage;
			var parentLi =  event.data.parentLi;

			backLink.style.display = "block";
			backImage.style.display = "block";
			popLink.style.display = "none";
			popImage.style.display = "none";

			backLink.style.zIndex = 1;
			backImage.style.zIndex = 1;
			popLink.style.zIndex = 1;
			popImage.style.zIndex = 1;
			parentLi.style.zIndex = 1;

  }

	function testPics(picarr){
		var index = null;
		var sum = 0;
		var maxLen = 11;
		var len = picarr.length<maxLen?picarr.length:maxLen;
		for(var i=0;i<len;i++){
			var item = picarr[i];
			if(item.height/item.width>1){
				if(index == null) index = i;
				sum++;
			}
		}
		if(sum/len>=0.5) return index;
		return -1;
	}

	function renderBig(pic,piclist,classId, rank){

		var height = 201;
		var w = pic.width*(height/pic.height);

		var li = document.createElement("li");

		li.id = "sogou_vr_"+classId+"_big_"+rank;
		li.style.position = "relative";
		li.className = "bigImg";
		li.style.width = w+"px";

		piclist.appendChild(li);

		return w;
	}

	function rebuildBig(elem, width ,height, item){
		var w = width;
		var h = height;
		var li = elem;
		var link = document.createElement("a");
		link.setAttribute("target","_blank");
		link.setAttribute("href",item.link);
        link.style.overflow = "hidden";
        link.style.display = "block";
		link.style.zIndex  = 1;

		li.style.width = w+"px";
		li.style.height = h+"px";
		img = imageFactory(item, w, h);
		img.setAttribute("src",item.src);
		link.appendChild(img);
		li.appendChild(link);

		  var pop_width = width*1.25+"px";
			var pop_height = height*1.25+"px";
			var pop_left = (0-width*0.1)+"px";
			var pop_top = (0-height*0.1)+"px";

			var link2 = document.createElement("a");
			link2.setAttribute("target","_blank");
			link2.setAttribute("href",item.link);
      link2.setAttribute("style","display:none;position:absolute;width:"+pop_width+";height:"+pop_height+";top:"+pop_top+";left:"+pop_left+";");
      link2.setAttribute("pop_width",pop_width);
	    link2.setAttribute("pop_height",pop_height);
	    link2.setAttribute("pop_left",pop_left);
	    link2.setAttribute("pop_top",pop_top);
	    link2.style.display = "none";

			var img2 = imageFactory(item, w, h);
			img2.setAttribute("src",item.src);
			img2.setAttribute("style","display:none;position:absolute;width:"+w+"px;height:"+h+"px;top:0px;left:0px;");
			img2.style.display = "none";
			link2.appendChild(img2);
			li.appendChild(link2);

			var param = {"backLink":link,"backImage":img,"popLink":link2,"popImage":img2,"parentLi":li};
			var userAgent = window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			if(!(/msie 6\.0/i.test(userAgent) || /msie 7\.0/i.test(userAgent)))
				$(li).bind("mouseenter",param,showPop).bind("mouseleave",param,hidePop);


	}

	function filter(picarr){
		var res = [];
		for(var i=0;i<picarr.length;i++){
			var item = picarr[i];
			if(item.width != 0 && item.height != 0)
				res.push(item);
		}
		return res;
	}

	return function(tplId, classId, rank, picarr,isIpad){

		var piclist = $s.$("sogou_vr_"+classId+"_piclist_"+rank);
		var num = piclist.getAttribute("data-num") || 1;

		num = +num;
		//num = 2;

		var start = 0, width, sumH = 0;
		if(isIpad == "ipad"){
			width=$($s.$("vr_"+rank)).find(".vrPicBox").width()
		}else{
			width=549;
		}

		picarr = filter(picarr);

		if(num != 2){
			getPic(picarr, start, width, piclist,classId,rank);
		}
		else{
			var index = testPics(picarr);
			if(index != -1){
				var big = picarr.splice(index,1)[0];
				var w = renderBig(big,piclist,classId, rank);
				width = width - w - 1;
			}
			for(var i=0;i<num;i++){
				var res = getPic(picarr, start, width, piclist,classId, rank);
				start = res.index;
				sumH += res.height;
			}
			var bigPic = $s.$("sogou_vr_"+classId+"_big_"+rank);
			if(bigPic){
				rebuildBig(bigPic, w ,sumH+1, big);
			}
		}

		var span = $s.$("sogou_vr_"+classId+"_num_"+rank);
		var t = $s.$("sogou_vr_"+classId+"_total_"+rank);
		if(span){
			var total = span.getAttribute("data-num");
			if(total.length > 3){
				total = total.replace(/(\d{3})(\d+)/,function(str,p1,p2){
					var zero = [];
					for(var i=0;i<p2.length;i++){
						zero.push("0");
					}
					return p1+zero.join("");
				});
				t.innerHTML = "张图片";
			}
			total = total.split("").reverse().join("");
			total = total.replace(/\d{3}/g,function(s){return s+","}).replace(/,$/,"");
			total = total.split("").reverse().join("");
			span.innerHTML = total;
		}

	}

});

<h3 class="vrTitle">

	function vrImgHandleLoad552(obj,width,height){
	 	calImg(obj);
	 	obj.style.visibility = "visible";
		function calImg (that){
			if (that.height == 0){
				setTimeout(function (){
					calImg(that);
				}, 50);
				return;
			}
			if(width != that.width){
				var pos = Math.floor((that.width - width)/2);
				obj.style.marginLeft = (-pos) + "px";
			}
			if(height != that.height){
				var pos = Math.floor((that.height - height)/2);
				obj.style.marginTop = (-pos) + "px";
			}
		}
	}

	function vrImgHandleError552(obj,width,height){
		var defaultImage = '/images/wx/120-80.png';
		if (width == 57) {
			defaultImage = '/images/wx/56-56.png';

			defaultImage = '/images/wx/88-88.png';
		} else if (width == 120) {
			defaultImage = '/images/wx/120-80.png';

			obj.parentNode.parentNode.style.display = "none";
		}
		obj.src=defaultImage;
		obj.style.visibility = "visible";
		obj.style.marginLeft = "0px";
		obj.style.marginTop = "0px";
	}

	function vrTimeHandle552(time){
		if (time) {
			var type = ["1分钟前", "分钟前", "小时前", "天前", "周前", "个月前", "年前"], secs = now/1000 - parseInt(time,10);
			if(secs < 60){
				return type[0];
			}else if(secs < 3600){
				return Math.floor(secs/60) + type[1];
			}else if(secs < 24*3600){
				return Math.floor(secs/3600) + type[2];
			}else if(secs < 24*3600 *7){
				return Math.floor(secs/(24*3600)) + type[3];
			}else if(secs < 24*3600*31){
				return Math.round(secs/(24*3600*7)) + type[4];
			}else if(secs < 24*3600*365){
				return Math.round(secs/(24*3600*31)) + type[5];
			}else if(secs >= 24*3600*365){
				return Math.round(secs/(24*3600*365)) + type[6];
			}else {
				return '';
			}
		} else {
			return '';
		}
	}

	function vrUrl552(that, q){

	function len(str){
		if(str)
				return str.replace(/<.*?>/g, "").replace(/[^\x00-\xff]/g,"rr").replace(/&nbsp;/g, " ").length;
		return 0;
	}
	function cutLength(str, maxLen, appended, appendLength){
		appended = appended||"...";
		appendLength = appendLength||2;
		str = str.replace(/<!.*?>/g, "");
		if (len(str) > maxLen){
			do{
				str = str.substring(0, str.length-1);
			}while(str && (len(str)+appendLength > maxLen));
			if (str.lastIndexOf("</") != str.lastIndexOf("<")){
				str = str.substring(0, str.lastIndexOf("<"))+str.substring(str.lastIndexOf(">")+1);
			}
			return str+appended;
		}
		return str;
	}

				return "";
			return obj.firstChild.nodeValue;
	}
